         // $('#back-to-top').tooltip('show');
 
 
             jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
 
 
                   // GREEN
                   // var navbarColor = "0,89,36";//color attr for rgba
                   // var navbarActiveColor = "0,62,25";//color attr for rgba
 
                   // BLUE
                   var navbarColor = "71,115,163";//color attr for rgba
                   var navbarActiveColor = "55,90,127";//color attr for rgba
 
                   // var navbarColor = "40,65,91";//color attr for rgba
                   // var navbarActiveColor = "40,65,91";//color attr for rgba
                   var navbarLangColor = "32,52,72";//color attr for rgba
                   var navbarSupportColor = "221,51,51";//color attr for rgba
                   var smallLogoHeight = jQuery('.small-logo').height();
                   var bigLogoHeight = jQuery('.big-logo').height();
                   var navbarHeight = jQuery('.navbar').height(); 
                   
                   var smallLogoEndPos = 0;
                   // var smallSpeed = (smallLogoHeight / bigLogoHeight);
 
                   var smallSpeed = 0.45;
                   
                   var ySmall = (jQuery(window).scrollTop() * smallSpeed); 
                   
                   var smallPadding = navbarHeight - ySmall;
                   if (smallPadding > navbarHeight) { smallPadding = navbarHeight; }
                   if (smallPadding < smallLogoEndPos) { smallPadding = smallLogoEndPos; }
                   if (smallPadding < 0) { smallPadding = 0; }
                   
                   jQuery('.small-logo-container ').css({ "padding-top": smallPadding});
                   
                   var navOpacity = ySmall / smallLogoHeight; 
                   if  (navOpacity > 1) { navOpacity = 1; }
                   if (navOpacity < 0 ) { navOpacity = 0; }
                   var navBackColor = 'rgba(' + navbarColor + ',' + navOpacity + ')';
                   jQuery('.navbar').css({"background-color": navBackColor});
 
                   var navActiveBackColor = 'rgba(' + navbarActiveColor + ',' + navOpacity + ')';
                   var navActiveBackColorNoScroll = 'rgba(' + navbarActiveColor + ',0.6)';
                   jQuery('#menu-primary-navigation>li.active').css({"background-color": navActiveBackColor});
 
                   var navLangBackColor = 'rgba(' + navbarLangColor + ',' + navOpacity + ')';
 
                   var navSupportBackColor = 'rgba(' + navbarSupportColor + ',' + navOpacity + ')';
 
                   var shadowOpacity = navOpacity * 0.4;
                   if ( ySmall > 1) {
                     jQuery('#cta-fixed-header-desktop').css({"box-shadow": "0 2px 3px rgba(0,0,0," + shadowOpacity + ")"});

   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {  
 
             jQuery(document).on("click",".list-btn",function(event) {
                 event.preventDefault();
 
                 jQuery('.image-list-item').removeClass('col-md-3 col-sm-6 col-xs-6 item-imagewrapper');
                 jQuery('.image-list-item').addClass('col-xs-12 item-listwrapper');
 
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts').removeClass('posts-list-imagewrapper');
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts').addClass('posts-list-listwrapper');
 
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts .posts-item-wrapper').removeClass('ImageWrapper');
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts .posts-item-wrapper').addClass('ListWrapper');
 
                 jQuery('.grid-btn').removeClass('active');
                 jQuery('.list-btn').addClass('active');
 
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on("click",".grid-btn",function(event) {
                 event.preventDefault();
 
                 jQuery('.image-list-item').removeClass('col-xs-12 item-listwrapper');
                 jQuery('.image-list-item').addClass('col-md-3 col-sm-6 col-xs-6 item-imagewrapper');
                 
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts').removeClass('posts-list-listwrapper');
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts').addClass('posts-list-imagewrapper');
 
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts .posts-item-wrapper').removeClass('ListWrapper');
                 jQuery('.list-grid-posts .posts-item-wrapper').addClass('ImageWrapper');
      
                 jQuery('.list-btn').removeClass('active');
                 jQuery('.grid-btn').addClass('active');
 
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on('mouseenter','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeOut(250);
                // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeOut(250);
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on('mouseleave','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeIn(250);
                // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeIn(250);
             });
             /*
             jQuery(document).on('focusin','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeOut(250);
                // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeOut(250);
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on('focusout','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeIn(250);
                // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeIn(250);
             });
             */
             jQuery( ".ImageWrapper" )
                 .focusout(function() {
                     jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeOut(250);
                 })
                 .focusin(function() {
                     jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-title').fadeIn(250);
                 });
 
             jQuery(document).on('mouseenter','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                jQuery(this).find('.caption').fadeOut(250);
                jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-content_type_badge').fadeOut(250);
                
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on('mouseleave','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                 jQuery(this).find('.caption').fadeIn(250);
                 jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-content_type_badge').fadeIn(250);
             });
 
                 jQuery(document).on('focusin','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                 jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-content_type_badge').fadeOut(250);
                 // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeOut(250);
             });
 
             jQuery(document).on('focusout','.ImageWrapper', function(){
                 jQuery(this).find('.posts-item-content_type_badge').fadeIn(250);
                 // jQuery(this).find('.content_type_badge').fadeIn(250);
             });
         
         });
   </script>

           China’s Impeding Internet Censorship Removes Thousands of Social Media Accounts
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="htc-date">
          June 15, 2018
         </div>
         <div class="htc-excerpt">
          In its continued effort to control and limit online speech, China has deleted 5,450 Sina Weibo accounts, the Chinese version of Twitter. According to a news report on Global Times this week, the action was taken against "posts that spread harmful information about current politics" on Sina Weibo. Sina Weibo is one of the biggest social media platforms in China.

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">

               <div class="posts-item-meta-item" style="display:block;padding-bottom:2px;">
                Posted in
                <a class="index-post-meta-link" href="http://tibet.net/announcements/department-diir-announcements/" style="" title="Department of Information &amp; International Relations">
                 Department of Information &amp; International Relations
                </a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               August 2018, Dharamshala On registration basis only The Department of Information and International Relations of Central Tibetan Administration is convening a Five-Fifty Youth Forum: Shaping Tibet’s Future, that will bring together a select group of 100 young Tibetans of the age group 25-40, from across the globe to discuss and deliberate on CTA’s Five-Fifty Vision.

          <script>
           var videosURL = "https://www.googleapis.com/youtube/v3/playlistItems?playlistId=UUQG1iEjZPBw9m4HSZgyVoUg&key=AIzaSyD889FiZZck8j3R4aiF8IbWQ6nvh0iATw0&fields=items&part=snippet&maxResults=20&callback=?";
 
             $.getJSON(videosURL, function(data) {
 
             var vidout;
             vidout = '';   
 
             $.each(data.items, function(i,val) {
 
             // console.log(val.snippet.title);
             // console.log(val.snippet.resourceId.videoId);
             // console.log(val.snippet.publishedAt); 
             // console.log(val.snippet.description);
             // console.log(val.snippet.thumbnails.default.url); 
 
 
             var date = new Date(val.snippet.publishedAt);
             var options = {
                 weekday: "long", year: "numeric", month: "short",
                 day: "numeric", hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit"
             };
 
             var fdate = date.toLocaleDateString("en-US");
             // var fdate = date.toLocaleTimeString("en-us", options));
            
 
             var jackbox1;
             jackbox1 = '<a id="vid-' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId + '-link"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' class="jackbox"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' style="display:block"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-group="tibet-tv"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-thumbnail="' + val.snippet.thumbnails.high.url + '"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-title="' + val.snippet.title + '"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-description="#description_' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId + '"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-thumbTooltip="' + val.snippet.description + '"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' data-autoplay="true"';
             jackbox1 = jackbox1 + ' href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId  + '">';
             
             var jackbox2;
             jackbox2 = '<a id="vid-' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId + '-link2"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' class="jackbox"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' style="display:inline"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-group="tibet-tv2"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-thumbnail="' + val.snippet.thumbnails.high.url + '"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-title="' + val.snippet.title + '"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-description="#description_' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId + '"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-thumbTooltip="' + val.snippet.description + '"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' data-autoplay="true"';
             jackbox2 = jackbox2 + ' href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=' + val.snippet.resourceId.videoId  + '">';
             
             vidout = vidout + '<li class="image-list-item col-xs-12 item-listwrapper">';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="posts-item posts-item-video">';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="posts-item-wrapper ListWrapper">';
             vidout = vidout + '<img alt="' + val.snippet.title + '" class="list-item-image img-responsive" src="' + val.snippet.thumbnails.high.url + '">';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="posts-item-title">';
             vidout = vidout + jackbox1;
             vidout = vidout + '<h4>' + val.snippet.title + '</h4>';
             vidout = vidout + '</a>';
             vidout = vidout + '</div>';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="posts-item-meta">';
             vidout = vidout + ' <div class="posts-item-meta-item">' + fdate + '</div>';
             vidout = vidout + '</div>';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="posts-item-excerpt">';
             vidout = vidout + val.snippet.description + jackbox2 + '&nbsp;View <i class="fa fa-angle-double-right"></i></a>';
             // vidout = vidout + jackbox2;
             // vidout = vidout + '&nbsp;View <i class="fa fa-angle-double-right"></i>';
             // vidout = vidout + '</a>';
             vidout = vidout + '</div>'; 
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="ImageOverlayH"></div>';
             vidout = vidout + '<div class="clearfix"></div>';

             vidout = vidout + '</div>  <!-- end .posts-item -->';
             vidout = vidout + '</li> <!-- end .image-list-item -->';
 
                 });
 
             document.getElementById('home-video-list').innerHTML = vidout;
 
             });

              <div class="posts-item-title">
               <a class="posts-item-title-link" href="/2017/04/update-on-the-latest-self-immolation-protest-in-tibet/">
                <h4>
                 Update on the Latest Self-immolation Protest in Tibet
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                <div class="cta-mobile-share">
                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2017/04/update-on-the-latest-self-immolation-protest-in-tibet/" data-toggle="dropdown">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: The latest Tibetan self-immolater has been identified as Wangchuk Tseten, according to sources inside Tibet quoted by Tibetan media. Wangchuk Tseten, a 30 year old father of three from Asey Gyechak nomadic region in Ngagrong county, Kardze (incorporated into China's Sichuan province) set himself on fire on 15 April 2017.

              <div class="posts-item-title">
               <a class="posts-item-title-link" href="/2017/04/self-immolation-protest-reported-from-kardze-in-eastern-tibet/">
                <h4>
                 Self-immolation Protest Reported from Kardze in Eastern Tibet
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                April 15, 2017
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                •  Published By
                <a href="#" target="_self">
                 Jamphel Shonu
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                <div class="cta-mobile-share">
                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2017/04/self-immolation-protest-reported-from-kardze-in-eastern-tibet/" data-toggle="dropdown">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: A Tibetan monk has set himself on fire in protest against the Chinese government this afternoon, according to reports emanating out of Tibet. The self-immolation reportedly took place in Kardze (incorporated into China’s Sichuan province).
               <a class="posts-item-readmore" href="http://tibet.net/2017/04/self-immolation-protest-reported-from-kardze-in-eastern-tibet/">

              <a href="/2016/12/a-tibetan-self-immolates-in-tibet/">
               <img alt="A Tibetan self-immolates in Tibet" class="list-item-image img-responsive" data-src="/cta-thumbs/90972self-immolation-1-300x144_400x400.jpg" src="http://tibet.net/wp-content/themes/cta-official/assets/img/loader.gif"/>
              </a>
              <div class="posts-item-title">
               <a class="posts-item-title-link" href="/2016/12/a-tibetan-self-immolates-in-tibet/">
                <h4>
                 A Tibetan self-immolates in Tibet
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                December 8, 2016
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                •  Published By
                <a href="#" target="_self">
                 Jamphel Shonu
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                <div class="cta-mobile-share">
                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2016/12/a-tibetan-self-immolates-in-tibet/" data-toggle="dropdown">
                  <i class="fa fa-share-alt">
                  </i>
                 </a>
                 <ul class="dropdown-menu cta_index_noapishare">
                  <li>
                   <a class="mobile-share-btn btn-facebook noapishare_link" data-original-title="Facebook" data-service="facebook" href="#">
                    <i class="fa fa-facebook">
                    </i>
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a class="mobile-share-btn btn-twitter noapishare_link" data-original-title="Twitter" data-service="twitter" href="#">
                    <i class="fa fa-twitter">
                    </i>
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a class="mobile-share-btn btn-google-plus noapishare_link" data-original-title="Google+" data-service="google-plus" href="#">
                    <i class="fa fa-google-plus">
                    </i>
                   </a>
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: A Tibetan self-immolated at around 5 pm local time today (8 December) on the streets of Machu county in Tibet's Amdo Province. According to a video received, a body is seen engulfed in flames . A woman standing nearby is heard reciting prayers in the name of His Holiness the Dalai Lama. The video also shows police arriving at the scene and taking away the charred body.

               <a class="posts-item-title-link" href="/2015/07/tibetan-monk-burns-self-in-kyegudo-self-immolation-reaches-141/">
                <h4>
                 Tibetan Monk Burns Self in Kyegudo, Self-immolation Reaches 141
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                July 10, 2015
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                •  Published By
                <a href="#" target="_self">
                 Jamphel Shonu
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                <div class="cta-mobile-share">
                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2015/07/tibetan-monk-burns-self-in-kyegudo-self-immolation-reaches-141/" data-toggle="dropdown">

                  </i>
                 </a>

                </div>
               </div>

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: Sonam Tobgyal, a 26-year-old Tibetan monk from Kyegudo, set himself on fire at around 6 pm on 9 July at Gesar Square, Kyegudo in Yulshul Tibetan Autonomous Prefecture (Incorporated into China’s Qinghai Province) in protest against the repressive policies of the Chinese government in Tibet. Local Tibetans who witnessed the incident took him to a nearby hospital.

                <h4>
                 Woman Burns in Protest Against Chinese Repression, Total Self-Immolation Reaches 140
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">
                May 28, 2015
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2015/05/woman-burns-in-protest-against-chinese-repression-in-kanlho-total-self-immolation-reaches-140/" data-toggle="dropdown">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: Showing no respite in the spate of self-immolation protests against the Chinese government, a 36-year-old Tibetan woman died after setting herself on fire on Wednesday, 27 May. The woman, Sangye Tso burned herself in front of the local Chinese police headquarters in Chone County, Kanlho Tibetan Autonomous Prefecture (Incorporated into China’s Gansu Province).

                <h4>
                 Father of Four Sets Self on Fire in Tawu, dies (update)

              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: Tenzin Gyatso, a father of four children in his mid thirties, died after setting himself on fire around 8:00 p.m on 20 May in an apparent protest against the Chinese government’s repressive policies in Tibet. The fiery protest took place in Khangsar township of Tawu (Ch: Daofu) County, Kardze (Ganzi) Tibetan Autonomous Prefecture (incorporated into China’s Sichuan Province).

                <h4>
                 Tibetan Monk Arrested Over Self-immolation Links
                </h4>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="posts-item-meta">
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

                <a href="#" target="_self">
                 Jamphel Shonu
                </a>
               </div>
               <div class="posts-item-meta-item">

                 <a class="cta_index_share_link" data-sharelink="http://tibet.net/2015/05/tibetan-monk-arrested-over-alleged-link-to-self-immolation-protest/" data-toggle="dropdown">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: Chinese police detained Tswang Choephel, a Tibetan monk from Nyitso monastery in Tawu county, Kardze (Ch: Ganzi) Tibetan Autonomous Prefecture (incorporated into China’s Sichuan Province) at around 10:30 am on 18 May, media reports say. Chinese authorities have not disclosed the reason for the monk’s detention.

                </h4>

              <div class="posts-item-meta">

              <div class="posts-item-excerpt">
               DHARAMSHALA: The Department of Religion and Culture of the Central Tibetan Administration organised a prayer service yesterday for the Tibetan self-immolators, particularly Tibetan nun Yeshi Khando and Ney Kyab, who died after setting themselves on fire in protest against the repressive policies of the Chinese government on 8 and 16 April respectively.

She is the 137th Tibetan since 2009 to self-immolate in protest against the Chinese government's repressive policies in Tibet.
